const TC = ["top", "right", "bottom", "left"]

    left: "right",

    start: "end",
    end: "start"

    return jt(n, fr(r, s))

function Tn(n, r) {
    return typeof n == "function" ? n(r) : n

function _n(n) {
    return n.split("-")[0]
}
function Vo(n) {
    return n.split("-")[1]
}
function od(n) {
    return n === "x" ? "y" : "x"
}
function sd(n) {
    return n === "y" ? "height" : "width"
}
function pr(n) {
    return ["top", "bottom"].includes(_n(n)) ? "y" : "x"
}
function id(n) {
    return od(pr(n))
}
function AC(n, r, s) {
    s === void 0 && (s = !1);
    const i = Vo(n)
      , l = id(n)
      , c = sd(l);
    let f = l === "x" ? i === (s ? "end" : "start") ? "right" : "left" : i === "start" ? "bottom" : "top";
    return r.reference[c] > r.floating[c] && (f = Oa(f)),
    [f, Oa(f)]
}
function MC(n) {
    const r = Oa(n);
    return [Ic(n), r, Ic(r)]
}
function Ic(n) {
    return n.replace(/start|end/g, r => OC[r])
}
function IC(n, r, s) {
    const i = ["left", "right"]
      , l = ["right", "left"]
      , c = ["top", "bottom"]
      , f = ["bottom", "top"];
    switch (n) {
    case "top":
    case "bottom":
        return s ? r ? l : i : r ? i : l;
    case "left":
    case "right":
        return r ? c : f;
    default:
        return []
    }
}
function DC(n, r, s, i) {
    const l = Vo(n);
    let c = IC(_n(n), s === "start", i);
    return l && (c = c.map(f => f + "-" + l),
    r && (c = c.concat(c.map(Ic)))),
    c
}
function Oa(n) {
    return n.replace(/left|right|bottom|top/g, r => _C[r])
}
function LC(n) {
    return {
        top: 0,
        right: 0,
        bottom: 0,
        left: 0,
        ...n
    }

function yg(n) {
    return typeof n != "number" ? LC(n) : {
        top: n,
        right: n,
        bottom: n,
        left: n
    }

function Aa(n) {
    const {x: r, y: s, width: i, height: l} = n;
    return {
        width: i,
        height: l,
        top: s,
        left: r,
        right: r + i,
        bottom: s + l,

        y: s
    }
}
function om(n, r, s) {
    let {reference: i, floating: l} = n;
    const c = pr(r)
      , f = id(r)
      , p = sd(f)
      , g = _n(r)
      , y = c === "y"
      , S = i.x + i.width / 2 - l.width / 2
      , x = i.y + i.height / 2 - l.height / 2
      , E = i[p] / 2 - l[p] / 2;
    let P;
    switch (g) {
    case "top":
        P = {
            x: S,
            y: i.y - l.height
        };
        break;
    case "bottom":
        P = {
            x: S,
            y: i.y + i.height
        };
        break;
    case "right":
        P = {
            x: i.x + i.width,
            y: x
        };
        break;
    case "left":
        P = {
            x: i.x - l.width,
            y: x
        };
        break;
    default:
        P = {
            x: i.x,
            y: i.y
        }
    }
    switch (Vo(r)) {
    case "start":
        P[f] -= E * (s && y ? -1 : 1);
        break;
    case "end":
        P[f] += E * (s && y ? -1 : 1);
        break
    }
    return P
}

async function HC(n, r) {

function Xb(n, r) {
    const s = Math.abs(r.top - n.y)
      , i = Math.abs(r.bottom - n.y)
      , l = Math.abs(r.right - n.x)
      , c = Math.abs(r.left - n.x);
    switch (Math.min(s, i, l, c)) {
    case c:
        return "left";
    case l:
        return "right";
    case s:
        return "top";
    case i:
        return "bottom";
    default:
        throw new Error("unreachable")
    }
}
function Jb(n, r, s=5) {
    const i = [];
    switch (r) {
    case "top":
        i.push({
            x: n.x - s,
            y: n.y + s
        }, {
            x: n.x + s,
            y: n.y + s
        });
        break;
    case "bottom":
        i.push({
            x: n.x - s,
            y: n.y - s
        }, {
            x: n.x + s,
            y: n.y - s
        });
        break;
    case "left":
        i.push({
            x: n.x + s,
            y: n.y - s
        }, {
            x: n.x + s,
            y: n.y + s
        });
        break;
    case "right":
        i.push({
            x: n.x - s,
            y: n.y - s
        }, {
            x: n.x - s,
            y: n.y + s
        });
        break
    }
    return i
}
function Zb(n) {
    const {top: r, right: s, bottom: i, left: l} = n;
    return [{
        x: l,
        y: r
    }, {
        x: s,
        y: r
    }, {
        x: s,
        y: i
    }, {
        x: l,
        y: i
    }]
}
function eE(n, r) {
    const {x: s, y: i} = n;
    let l = !1;
    for (let c = 0, f = r.length - 1; c < r.length; f = c++) {
        const p = r[c].x
          , g = r[c].y
          , y = r[f].x
          , S = r[f].y;
        g > i != S > i && s < (y - p) * (i - g) / (S - g) + p && (l = !l)
    }
    return l
}
function tE(n) {
    const r = n.slice();
    return r.sort( (s, i) => s.x < i.x ? -1 : s.x > i.x ? 1 : s.y < i.y ? -1 : s.y > i.y ? 1 : 0),
    nE(r)
}
function nE(n) {
    if (n.length <= 1)
        return n.slice();
    const r = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < n.length; i++) {
        const l = n[i];
        for (; r.length >= 2; ) {
            const c = r[r.length - 1]
              , f = r[r.length - 2];
            if ((c.x - f.x) * (l.y - f.y) >= (c.y - f.y) * (l.x - f.x))
                r.pop();
            else
                break
        }
        r.push(l)
    }
    r.pop();
    const s = [];
    for (let i = n.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        const l = n[i];
        for (; s.length >= 2; ) {
            const c = s[s.length - 1]
              , f = s[s.length - 2];
            if ((c.x - f.x) * (l.y - f.y) >= (c.y - f.y) * (l.x - f.x))
                s.pop();
            else
                break
        }
        s.push(l)
    }
    return s.pop(),
    r.length === 1 && s.length === 1 && r[0].x === s[0].x && r[0].y === s[0].y ? r : r.concat(s)
}

async function Yg(n) {
    if (!n.ok) {
        const r = n.headers.get("content-type");
        if (r && r.includes("application/json")) {
            const s = await n.json();
            throw new Error(s.message || `${n.status}: ${n.statusText}`)
        } else
            throw await n.text(),
            new Error(`${n.status}: ${n.statusText}`)
    }
}
async function zc(n, r, s) {
    const i = localStorage.getItem("token")
      , l = await fetch(r, {
        method: n,
        headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            Authorization: `Bearer ${i}`
        },
        body: s ? JSON.stringify(s) : void 0,
        credentials: "include"
    });
    return await Yg(l),
    l
}
const zE = ({on401: n}) => async ({queryKey: r}) => {

}

function $E() {
    const {toast: n} = Uo()
      , [r,s] = v.useState(!1)
      , i = async () => {
        var l, c;
        try {
            s(!0);
            const f = await zc("POST", "/api/payments/subscribe", {
                headers: {
                    Accept: "application/json",
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                },
                credentials: "include",
                mode: "cors"
            });
            let p;
            try {
                p = await f.json()
            } catch (y) {
                throw console.error("Response parsing error:", y),
                new Error("Failed to parse server response")
            }
            if (!f.ok || !p)
                throw new Error((p == null ? void 0 : p.message) || `Payment request failed (${f.status})`);
            if (!p.url)
                throw new Error("Payment URL not received");
            if (!f.ok) {
                const y = (p == null ? void 0 : p.message) || "Payment session creation failed";
                throw console.error("Server error:", {
                    status: f.status,
                    message: y
                }),
                new Error(y)
            }
            if (!p.url)
                throw new Error("Payment URL not received");
            if (console.log("Stripe URL:", p.url),
            !window.open(p.url, "_self"))
                throw new Error("Failed to open Stripe checkout. Please enable popups and try again.")
        } catch (f) {
            console.error("Payment initiation error:", f);
            let p = "Failed to initiate subscription. Please try again.";
            (l = f.message) != null && l.includes("configuration") ? p = "Payment system configuration error. Please try again later." : (c = f.message) != null && c.includes("network") && (p = "Network error. Please check your connection and try again."),
            n({
                variant: "destructive",
                title: "Payment Error",
                description: p
            }),
            s(!1)
        }
    }
    ;
    return h.jsx("div", {
        className: "space-y-4",
        children: h.jsxs(mr, {
            children: [h.jsx(Js, {
                children: h.jsx(Zs, {
                    children: "Premium Plan"

            secondary: "border-transparent bg-secondary text-secondary-foreground hover:bg-secondary/80",
            destructive: "border-transparent bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground hover:bg-destructive/80",
            outline: "text-foreground"
        }
    },
    defaultVariants: {
        variant: "default"
    }
});
function uk({className: n, variant: r, ...s}) {
    return h.jsx("div", {
        className: ue(lk({
            variant: r
        }), n),
        ...s
    })
}
class ck {
    static async generate(r) {
        const s = window.open("", "_blank");
        if (!s)
            return;
        const i = `
      <!DOCTYPE html>
      <html>
        <head>
          <title>${r.planId} - Job Plan</title>
          <style>
            body {
              font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
              line-height: 1.6;
              margin: 40px;
            }
            h1 { margin-bottom: 20px; }
            h2 { margin-top: 20px; color: #666; }
            .section { margin-bottom: 20px; }
            .grid { display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr; gap: 10px; }
            @media print {
              body { margin: 20px; }
            }
          </style>
        </head>
        <body>
          <h1>${r.planId} - Maintenance Job Plan</h1>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Equipment Details</h2>
            <div class="grid">
              <div>Name: ${r.equipmentName}</div>
              <div>Model: ${r.equipmentModel || "N/A"}</div>
              <div>Serial: ${r.equipmentSerial || "N/A"}</div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Scope of Work</h2>
            <p>${r.scopeOfWork}</p>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Job Steps</h2>
            ${r.jobSteps.map( (l, c) => `
              <div style="margin-bottom: 20px;">
                <h3>Step ${l.stepNumber || c + 1}</h3>
                <p>${l.description}</p>
              </div>
            `).join("")}
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Tools & Materials</h2>
            <div class="grid">
              <div>
                <strong>Tools Required:</strong>
                <ul>
                  ${r.toolsRequired.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
                </ul>
              </div>
              <div>
                <strong>Materials Required:</strong>
                <ul>
                  ${r.materialsRequired.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
                </ul>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Manpower</h2>
            <div>Count: ${r.manpowerCount}</div>
            <div>Skills: ${r.skillLevels.join(", ")}</div>
            <div>Estimated Time: ${r.estimatedTime}</div>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Safety Requirements</h2>
            <div>
              <strong>PPE:</strong>
              <ul>
                ${r.safetyPpe.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
              </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
              <strong>Safety Procedures:</strong>
              <ul>
                ${r.safetyProcedures.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
              </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
              <strong>Potential Hazards:</strong>
              <ul>
                ${r.safetyHazards.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
              </ul>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Best Practices</h2>
            <p>${r.bestPractices}</p>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Recommendations</h2>
            <div>
              <strong>Manuals:</strong>
              <ul>
                ${r.recommendations.manuals.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
              </ul>
            </div>
            <div>
              <strong>Procedures:</strong>
              <ul>
                ${r.recommendations.procedures.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
              </ul>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="section">
            <h2>Applicable Codes & Standards</h2>
            <ul>
              ${r.applicableCodes.map(l => `<li>${l}</li>`).join("")}
            </ul>
          </div>

          ${"notes"in r && r.notes ? `
          <div class="section">
            <h2>Notes</h2>
            <p>${r.notes}</p>
          </div>
          ` : ""}
        </body>
      </html>
    `;
        s.document.write(i),
        s.document.close(),
        s.onload = () => {
            s.print()
        }
    }
}
function vy({plan: n}) {
    const [r,s] = v.useState(!0)
      , [i,l] = v.useState(n)
      , {toast: c} = Uo()
      , f = (b, w="") => {
        Array.isArray(i[b]) && l({
            ...i,
            [b]: [...i[b], w]
        })
    }
      , p = (b, w) => {
        Array.isArray(i[b]) && l({
            ...i,
            [b]: i[b].filter( (C, j) => j !== w)
        })
    }
      , g = () => {
        const b = {
            stepNumber: i.jobSteps.length + 1,
            description: ""
        };
        l({
            ...i,
            jobSteps: [...i.jobSteps, b]
        })
    }
      , y = b => {
        l({
            ...i,
            jobSteps: i.jobSteps.filter( (w, C) => C !== b)
        })
    }
      , S = b => {
        l({
            ...i,
            recommendations: {
                ...i.recommendations,
                [b]: [...i.recommendations[b], ""]
            }
        })
    }
      , x = (b, w) => {
        l({
            ...i,
            recommendations: {
                ...i.recommendations,
                [b]: i.recommendations[b].filter( (C, j) => j !== w)
            }
        })
    }
      , E = ja({
        mutationFn: async b => (await zc("id"in b ? "PATCH" : "POST", "id"in b ? `/api/job-plans/${b.id}` : "/api/job-plans", b)).json(),
        onSuccess: () => {
            fm.invalidateQueries({
                queryKey: ["/api/job-plans"]
            }),
            c({
                title: "Success",
                description: "Job plan saved successfully"
            }),
            s(!1)
        }
        ,
        onError: b => {
            c({
                variant: "destructive",
                title: "Error",
                description: b.message
            })
        }
    })
      , P = ja({
        mutationFn: async b => {
            await zc("DELETE", `/api/job-plans/${b}`)
        }
        ,
        onSuccess: () => {
            fm.invalidateQueries({
                queryKey: ["/api/job-plans"]
            }),
            c({
                title: "Success",
                description: "Job plan deleted successfully"
            })
        }
        ,
        onError: b => {
            c({
                variant: "destructive",
                title: "Error",
                description: b.message
            })
        }
    });
    return h.jsxs(mr, {
        children: [h.jsxs(Js, {
            className: "flex flex-row items-center justify-between",
            children: [h.jsxs(Zs, {
                className: "text-2xl",
                children: [n.planId, " ", h.jsx(uk, {
                    variant: "outline",
                    className: "ml-2",
                    children: "status"in n ? n.status : "draft"
                })]
            }), h.jsxs("div", {
                className: "flex gap-2",
                children: ["id"in n && h.jsx(Se, {
                    variant: "destructive",
                    size: "sm",
                    onClick: () => P.mutate(n.id),
                    children: h.jsx(RS, {
                        className: "h-4 w-4"
                    })
                }), h.jsx(Se, {
                    variant: "outline",
                    size: "sm",
                    onClick: () => ck.generate(n),
                    children: h.jsx(SS, {
                        className: "h-4 w-4"
                    })
                }), h.jsx(Se, {
                    variant: "default",
                    size: "sm",
                    onClick: () => E.mutate(i),
                    children: h.jsx(NS, {
                        className: "h-4 w-4"
                    })
                })]
            })]
        }), h.jsx(vr, {
            children: h.jsxs(my, {
                type: "multiple",
                defaultValue: ["equipment", "scope", "steps", "tools", "manpower", "safety", "practices", "codes"],
                children: [h.jsxs(pt, {
                    value: "equipment",
                    children: [h.jsx(ht, {
                        children: "Equipment Details"
                    }), h.jsx(mt, {
                        children: h.jsxs("div", {
                            className: "space-y-4",
                            children: [h.jsx(Be, {
                                value: i.equipmentName,
                                onChange: b => l({
                                    ...i,
                                    equipmentName: b.target.value
                                }),
                                placeholder: "Equipment Name"
                            }), h.jsx(Be, {
                                value: i.equipmentModel,
                                onChange: b => l({
                                    ...i,
                                    equipmentModel: b.target.value
                                }),
                                placeholder: "Model"
                            }), h.jsx(Be, {
                                value: i.equipmentSerial,
                                onChange: b => l({
                                    ...i,
                                    equipmentSerial: b.target.value
                                }),
                                placeholder: "Serial Number"
                            })]
                        })
                    })]
                }), h.jsxs(pt, {
                    value: "scope",
                    children: [h.jsx(ht, {
                        children: "Scope of Work"
                    }), h.jsx(mt, {
                        children: h.jsx($s, {
                            value: i.scopeOfWork,
                            onChange: b => l({
                                ...i,

                            className: "min-h-[100px]"

                                        value: b,
                                        onChange: C => {
                                            const j = [...i.recommendations.procedures];
                                            j[w] = C.target.value,
                                            l({
                                                ...i,
                                                recommendations: {
                                                    ...i.recommendations,
                                                    procedures: j
                                                }
                                            })
                                        }
                                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                                        type: "button",
                                        variant: "ghost",
                                        size: "icon",
                                        onClick: () => x("procedures", w),
                                        children: h.jsx(Ft, {
                                            className: "h-4 w-4"
                                        })
                                    })]
                                }, w))]
                            })]
                        })
                    })]
                }), h.jsxs(pt, {
                    value: "codes",
                    children: [h.jsx(ht, {
                        children: h.jsxs("div", {
                            className: "flex justify-between items-center w-full pr-4",
                            children: [h.jsx("span", {
                                children: "Applicable Codes & Standards"
                            }), h.jsxs(Se, {
                                type: "button",
                                variant: "outline",
                                size: "sm",
                                onClick: b => {
                                    b.stopPropagation(),
                                    f("applicableCodes")
                                }
                                ,
                                children: [h.jsx(ln, {
                                    className: "h-4 w-4 mr-2"
                                }), "Add Code"]
                            })]
                        })
                    }), h.jsx(mt, {
                        children: h.jsx("div", {
                            className: "space-y-2",
                            children: i.applicableCodes.map( (b, w) => h.jsxs("div", {
                                className: "flex gap-2",
                                children: [h.jsx(Be, {
                                    value: b,
                                    onChange: C => {
                                        const j = [...i.applicableCodes];
                                        j[w] = C.target.value,
                                        l({
                                            ...i,
                                            applicableCodes: j
                                        })
                                    }
                                }), h.jsx(Se, {
                                    type: "button",
                                    variant: "ghost",
                                    size: "icon",
                                    onClick: () => p("applicableCodes", w),
                                    children: h.jsx(Ft, {
                                        className: "h-4 w-4"
                                    })
                                })]
                            }, w))
                        })
                    })]
                })]
            })
        })]
    })
}
function dk() {
    const [n,r] = v.useState("")
      , {toast: s} = Uo()
      , [i,l] = v.useState(3)
      , c = ja({
        mutationFn: async f => {
            const p = localStorage.getItem("token");
            if (!p)
                throw new Error("Please login first");
            const g = await fetch("/api/job-plans/generate", {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                    Authorization: `Bearer ${p}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    query: f
                })
            });
            if (!g.ok) {
                const y = await g.json();
                throw new Error(y.message || "Failed to generate plan")
            }
            return g.json()
        }
        ,
        onError: f => {
            s({
                title: "Error",
                description: f.message,
                variant: "destructive"
            })
        }
    });
    return h.jsxs("div", {
        className: "space-y-6",
        children: [h.jsx("h1", {
            className: "text-3xl font-bold text-center",
            children: "AI Maintenance Planner"
        }), h.jsx("div", {
            className: "max-w-3xl mx-auto text-center",
            children: h.jsx("p", {
                className: "text-lg text-muted-foreground",
                children: "AI Maintenance Planner helps you build a detailed document that outlines the specific tasks, resources, and timelines required to maintain equipment effectively. Just enter the scope of work and let the AI planner build you a custom job plan in seconds."
            })
        }), h.jsx(mr, {
            className: "mb-6",
            children: h.jsx(vr, {
                className: "pt-6",
                children: h.jsxs("div", {
                    className: "text-center mb-6",
                    children: [h.jsx("h2", {
                        className: "text-2xl font-bold mb-2",
                        children: "Sample Job Plan"
                    }), h.jsx("p", {
                        className: "text-muted-foreground",
                        children: "View our sample job plan to see how our AI creates detailed, professional maintenance plans"
                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                        variant: "outline",
                        className: "mt-4 hover:bg-[rgb(0,85,255)] hover:text-white",
                        onClick: () => window.open("/MJP-2025-0641 - Job Plan.pdf"),
                        children: "View Sample Plan"
                    })]
                })
            })
        }), h.jsx(mr, {
            children: h.jsxs(vr, {
                className: "pt-6",
                children: [h.jsxs("form", {
                    onSubmit: f => {
                        f.preventDefault(),
                        c.mutate(n)
                    }
                    ,
                    className: "flex gap-2",
                    children: [h.jsx(Be, {
                        value: n,
                        onChange: f => r(f.target.value),
                        placeholder: "Describe the maintenance task (e.g., Replace hydraulic pump on CNC lathe)",
                        className: "flex-1"
                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                        type: "submit",
                        disabled: c.isPending,
                        className: "bg-[rgb(255,255,255)] hover:bg-[rgb(0,85,255)]/90",
                        children: c.isPending ? h.jsxs(h.Fragment, {
                            children: [h.jsx(kv, {
                                className: "mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin"
                            }), "Generating..."]
                        }) : "Generate Plan"
                    })]
                }), i > 0 && h.jsxs("p", {
                    className: "mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center",
                    children: ["You have ", i, " free plan", i !== 1 && "s", " remaining today"]
                }), c.data && h.jsx("div", {
                    className: "mt-8",
                    children: h.jsx(vy, {
                        plan: c.data
                    })
                })]
            })
        })]
    })
}
function fk() {
    const {data: n, isLoading: r} = w0({
        queryKey: ["/api/job-plans"],
        queryFn: async () => {
            const s = await fetch("/api/job-plans", {
                headers: {
                    Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem("token")}`
                }
            });
            if (!s.ok)
                throw new Error("Failed to fetch job plans");
            return s.json()
        }
    });
    return r ? h.jsxs("div", {
        className: "space-y-4",
        children: [h.jsx(zs, {
            className: "h-8 w-48"
        }), h.jsx(zs, {
            className: "h-[200px] w-full"
        }), h.jsx(zs, {
            className: "h-[200px] w-full"
        })]
    }) : h.jsxs("div", {
        className: "max-w-4xl mx-auto",
        children: [h.jsx("h1", {
            className: "text-4xl font-bold mb-8",
            children: "Saved Job Plans"
        }), h.jsx("div", {
            className: "space-y-8",
            children: (n == null ? void 0 : n.length) === 0 ? h.jsx(mr, {
                children: h.jsx(vr, {
                    className: "pt-6",
                    children: h.jsx("p", {
                        className: "text-center text-muted-foreground",
                        children: "Saved Job plans not available on the free version."
                    })
                })
            }) : n == null ? void 0 : n.map(s => h.jsx(vy, {
                plan: s
            }, s.id))
        })]
    })
}
function pk() {
    const [n,r] = v.useState(!0)
      , [,s] = Vc()
      , {toast: i} = Uo()
      , {mutate: l} = ja({
        mutationFn: async f => {
            const p = await fetch(`/api/auth/${n ? "login" : "register"}`, {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                    Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem("token")}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(f)
            });
            if (!p.ok)
                throw new Error((await p.json()).message);
            return p.json()
        }
        ,
        onSuccess: f => {
            localStorage.setItem("token", f.token),
            i({
                title: n ? "Logged in successfully" : "Registered successfully"
            }),
            s("/")
        }
        ,
        onError: f => {
            i({
                title: "Error",
                description: f.message,
                variant: "destructive"
            })
        }
    })
      , c = f => {
        f.preventDefault();
        const p = new FormData(f.currentTarget)
          , g = Object.fromEntries(p);
        l(g)
    }
    ;
    return h.jsx("div", {
        className: "max-w-md mx-auto mt-20",
        children: h.jsxs(mr, {
            children: [h.jsx(Js, {
                children: h.jsx(Zs, {
                    children: n ? "Login" : "Register"
                })
            }), h.jsx(vr, {
                children: h.jsxs("form", {
                    onSubmit: c,
                    className: "space-y-4",
                    children: [!n && h.jsx(Be, {
                        name: "name",
                        placeholder: "Full Name",
                        required: !0
                    }), h.jsx(Be, {
                        name: "email",
                        type: "email",
                        placeholder: "Email",
                        required: !0
                    }), h.jsx(Be, {
                        name: "password",
                        type: "password",
                        placeholder: "Password",
                        required: !0
                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                        type: "submit",
                        className: "w-full",
                        children: n ? "Login" : "Register"
                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                        type: "button",
                        variant: "ghost",
                        className: "w-full",
                        onClick: () => r(!n),
                        children: n ? "Need an account? Register" : "Have an account? Login"
                    })]
                })
            })]
        })
    })
}

function mk() {
    const [n,r] = v.useState("")
      , [s,i] = v.useState("")
      , [l,c] = v.useState("")
      , {toast: f} = Uo()
      , p = async g => {
        g.preventDefault();
        try {
            if ((await fetch("/api/contact", {
                method: "POST",
                headers: {
                    "Content-Type": "application/json"
                },
                body: JSON.stringify({
                    name: n,
                    email: s,
                    message: l
                })
            })).ok)
                f({
                    title: "Success",
                    description: "Your message has been sent successfully."
                }),
                r(""),
                i(""),
                c("");
            else
                throw new Error("Failed to send message")
        } catch {
            f({
                title: "Error",
                description: "Failed to send message. Please try again.",
                variant: "destructive"
            })
        }
    }
    ;
    return h.jsx("div", {
        className: "max-w-2xl mx-auto mt-8",
        children: h.jsxs(mr, {
            children: [h.jsx(Js, {
                children: h.jsx(Zs, {
                    children: "Contact Us"
                })
            }), h.jsx(vr, {
                children: h.jsxs("form", {
                    onSubmit: p,
                    className: "space-y-4",
                    children: [h.jsx("div", {
                        children: h.jsx(Be, {
                            placeholder: "Your Name",
                            value: n,
                            onChange: g => r(g.target.value),
                            required: !0
                        })
                    }), h.jsx("div", {
                        children: h.jsx(Be, {
                            type: "email",
                            placeholder: "Your Email",
                            value: s,
                            onChange: g => i(g.target.value),
                            required: !0
                        })
                    }), h.jsx("div", {
                        children: h.jsx($s, {
                            placeholder: "Your Message",
                            value: l,
                            onChange: g => c(g.target.value),
                            className: "min-h-[150px]",
                            required: !0
                        })
                    }), h.jsx(Se, {
                        type: "submit",
                        className: "w-full",
                        children: "Send Message"
                    })]
                })
            })]
        })
    })
}
